16:45:25","updatedTime":"2020-09-05 16:45:25","title":"‘World of Death’ Films ‘House on the Lake’ and ‘Ding Dong’ Bring Vampires, Isolation, and Terror! [Watch]","link":"https://bloody-disgusting.com/?p=3628700","description":"<p>Hello out there all you loyal viewers!</p>\n<p>We hope everyone is doing well and performing their civic duties in every form and fashion. Today we have a couple shorts that embody both the approaching Halloween season and the isolation of the past six months in various forms. I like to think these couple of creature features are manifestations of all of our fears in 2020, lurking in the shadows, just waiting for the right time to pounce.</p>\n<p>The first one up is called <em><strong>The House on the Lake</strong></em>, coming from director <strong>Damien Kazan</strong>. Here, we have a story of a young woman at home alone in a seemingly isolated woodland area right on the lake. What could possibly go wrong? I&#8217;ll tell you what can go wrong. While going to the bathroom you start hearing strange knocks on the door, at your most vulnerable state. I love the tension building in this very simple &#8220;go check on the strange noises&#8221; horror trope.  We&#8217;ve seen it a million times before. However, sometimes it&#8217;s about how you do it, rather than what you did. The lighting and camera setups do a great job of telling the story in this one.</p>\n<p>The second short we have for you this month comes from director <strong>Timothy Troy</strong>, entitled <em><strong>Ding Dong</strong></em>. No, it&#8217;s not what you think&#8230;the popular chocolatey, cream-filled treat some of us spent time stuffing down our gullets during quarantine. I&#8217;m talking about the sound a doorbell makes when we&#8217;re all alone in our house trying to get into bed, scaring us half to death. That&#8217;s exactly what happens in this vignette. Poor Alexis just wants to get some damn sleep, but that just isn&#8217;t possible with someone ringing your doorbell every two minutes. Is it just the neighborhood kids screwing around? Or is it something far more sinister? I guess you&#8217;ll have to watch and find out.</p>\n<p>Stay safe out there, folks. Fall is approaching and it&#8217;s our time to shine. So get out your pumpkin-scented candles and big sweaters and cozy up to a good horror movie. We&#8217;ll do our part and offer up some appetizing options.</p>\n<p>&#8211; Dominick DeLuca</p>\n<p><iframe class='youtube-player' width='740' height='417' src='https://www.youtube.com/embed/R89NW7CetHs?version=3&#038;rel=1&#038;fs=1&#038;autohide=2&#038;showsearch=0&#038;showinfo=1&#038;iv_load_policy=1&#038;wmode=transparent' allowfullscreen='true' style='border:0;'></iframe></p>\n<p><a href=\"http://bloody-disgusting.com/wod\">World of Death</a> is the web series that fans of independent horror have been waiting for. Featuring short horror films from all over the globe created by the largest variety of talent that a collection has ever been able to boast, WOD provides plenty of blood, guts, screams and laughs for all fans of the macabre. WOD is the perfect entertainment for a fan base constantly on the go. Watch it anywhere, at any time, for FREE! meaning there could be no delay in bringing &#8220;Chucky&#8221; to his adoring fans.</p>\n<p>&#8220;Chucky&#8221; hails from franchise creator <strong>Don Mancini</strong> and “Channel Zero” mastermind <strong>Nick Antosca</strong>, and brings <a href=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/tv/3624564/brad-dourif-officially-confirmed-voice-chucky-upcoming-tv-series/\"><strong>Brad Dourif </strong>back to voice the possessed doll.</a></p>\n<p>&#8220;Chucky&#8221; has been described as a “fresh take on the franchise” that’ll “explore Chucky’s character with a depth that is uniquely afforded by the television series format.”</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 40px;\">“After a vintage Chucky doll turns up at a suburban yard sale, an idyllic American town is thrown into chaos as a series of horrifying murders begin to expose the town’s hypocrisies and secrets. Meanwhile, the arrival of enemies — and allies — from Chucky’s past threatens to expose the truth behind the killings, as well as the demon doll’s untold origins as a seemingly ordinary child who somehow became this notorious monster.”</p>\n<p>“<em><strong>With this TV show, our mission has been to preserve the straightforward scariness of the original film</strong> <strong>or the first couple of films</strong></em>,” <a href=\"https://www.syfy.com/syfywire/don-mancini-childs-play-watch-party-chucky-tv-show?fbclid=IwAR02lZkrdXFRnTYEX6zNni6k8WiDN7xzbesTkUFmh-mu6Q2ht_RfnvHyIHk\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Mancini explained to Syfy Wire back in May</a>. “<em>But at the same time, continue on with this ever-expanding tapestry of consistent story that we’ve spun over the course of seven movies and 30-some years.<strong> I think fans are really gonna love to see the new characters that we introduce into this realm</strong> and just to see how they came off of our classic characters. Not just Chucky, but <strong>some of the others that you may be hoping to see. There’s a good chance they may turn up</strong></em>.”</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/tv/3603920/jennifer-tilly-confirms-shell-part-syfy-don-mancinis-chucky-tv-series/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><strong>Jennifer Tilly</strong>, on that particular note, has already confirmed she’ll be back.</a></p>\n<p>Mancini also teased in his chat with Syfy Wire, “<em>I think the prospect of seeing Chucky sharpen his skills and add to his toolbox, some of the technical goodies that we have at our disposal now, that’s something I think people will find pretty interesting. It’s so important to give Chucky new weapons, new strategies, and new targets, new goals. <strong>Chucky has a different goal in the TV show than he’s ever had before and it’s specifically something that is designed to evoke something that’s going on in the zeitgeist today</strong></em>.”</p>\n<blockquote class=\"instagram-media\" style=\"background: #FFF; These films are made or broken by their own designs; story quality, sequence, and consistency are key criteria. The few examples that excel in all these areas are the paragons of segmented horror.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Although it&#8217;s true some of these movies fare better than others in the matter of overall quality, some lesser known anthologies clearly have a standout story that shouldn&#8217;t be missed.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>The House of the Dead</i></b><b> (1978) — &#8220;Miss Sibiler&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/The-House-of-the-Dead.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630553\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/the-house-of-the-dead/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/The-House-of-the-Dead.jpg?fit=1200%2C600&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,600\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"The-House-of-the-Dead\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/The-House-of-the-Dead.jpg?fit=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/The-House-of-the-Dead.jpg?fit=740%2C370&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630553\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/The-House-of-the-Dead.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/The-House-of-the-Dead.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/The-House-of-the-Dead.jpg?resize=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/The-House-of-the-Dead.jpg?resize=1024%2C512&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/The-House-of-the-Dead.jpg?resize=768%2C384&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This omnibus goes by several names: </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Alien Zone</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Five Faces of Terror</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, and </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Last Stop on 13th Street</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. Regardless of the title, </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The House of the Dead</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> is a curio among regional horrors. This attempt at an Amicus-style anthology was shot in Oklahoma with only a budget of $685,000; director and producer Sharron Miller made her feature debut here. David O&#8217;Malley&#8217;s script offers up five undercooked stories, but they are all memorable in their own right.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Following the wraparound where a mortician greets his late-night visitor, we meet a school teacher who hates children. Miss Sibiler&#8217;s animosity transforms into palpable fear, though, when a pack of kids in ghastly masks shows up at her house one fateful night. There&#8217;s no rhyme or reason to the feral tykes&#8217; sudden appearance, yet it&#8217;s a classic case of getting one&#8217;s comeuppance.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>Terror Tract</i></b><b> (2000) — &#8220;Come to Granny&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Terror-Tract.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630554\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/terror-tract/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Terror-Tract.jpg?fit=1200%2C600&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,600\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"Terror-Tract\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Terror-Tract.jpg?fit=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Terror-Tract.jpg?fit=740%2C370&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630554\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Terror-Tract.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Terror-Tract.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Terror-Tract.jpg?resize=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Terror-Tract.jpg?resize=1024%2C512&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Terror-Tract.jpg?resize=768%2C384&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Ardent viewers of USA Network may remember seeing this anthology during Shriek Week, a block of horror programming that aired around Halloween. Fans of </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Cherry Falls</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> will have spotted the movie on a two-for-one DVD. However, this dark comedy has slipped through the cracks and isn&#8217;t easy to come by. John Ritter plays a desperate real estate agent hoping to make a sale, or else more than his job will be at stake. Unfortunately, he&#8217;s done in by his own misguided strategy of showing his clients murder houses.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">In the case of the final story &#8220;Come to Granny,&#8221; no one was technically killed in the Goodwins&#8217; home. Still, the owners have since moved on because of a local spate of deaths that involved their son. This suburban slasher was likely inspired by </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Eyes of Laura Mars</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> seeing as the teen protagonist shares an unexplained psychic link with a serial killer nicknamed the Granny Killer. All in all, </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Terror Tract</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> is an entertaining look at disturbia.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>From a Whisper to a Scream</i></b><b> (1987) — &#8220;Stanley&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/From-a-Whisper-to-a-Scream.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630555\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/from-a-whisper-to-a-scream-2/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/From-a-Whisper-to-a-Scream.jpg?fit=1200%2C600&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,600\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"From-a-Whisper-to-a-Scream\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/From-a-Whisper-to-a-Scream.jpg?fit=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/From-a-Whisper-to-a-Scream.jpg?fit=740%2C370&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630555\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/From-a-Whisper-to-a-Scream.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/From-a-Whisper-to-a-Scream.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/From-a-Whisper-to-a-Scream.jpg?resize=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/From-a-Whisper-to-a-Scream.jpg?resize=1024%2C512&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/From-a-Whisper-to-a-Scream.jpg?resize=768%2C384&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Also known as </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The Offspring</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">From a Whisper to a Scream</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> boasts a distinguished cast that includes Vincent Price, Susan Tyrrell, and Cameron Mitchell. The movie&#8217;s Southern Gothic atmosphere is writ large, and every story takes place at a specific point in Tennessee&#8217;s history. Tyrrell plays a reporter who visits Price&#8217;s character, a historian recounting macabre tales of the Deep South.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The opening story sees its namesake committing terrible acts. Ultimately, Stanley&#8217;s misdeeds come back to bite him in the most literal way possible.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>Dead of Night</i></b><b> (1977) — &#8220;Bobby&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Dead-of-Night.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630556\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/dead-of-night-2/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Dead-of-Night.jpg?fit=1200%2C916&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,916\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"Dead-of-Night\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Dead-of-Night.jpg?fit=300%2C229&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Dead-of-Night.jpg?fit=740%2C565&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630556\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Dead-of-Night.jpg?resize=740%2C565&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"565\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Dead-of-Night.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Dead-of-Night.jpg?resize=300%2C229&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Dead-of-Night.jpg?resize=1024%2C782&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Dead-of-Night.jpg?resize=768%2C586&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Dan Curtis, the mastermind behind </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Dark Shadows</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, followed up on his popular telefilm </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Trilogy of Terror</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> with another anthology. And like before, famed genre author and screenwriter Richard Matheson was involved. His story &#8220;Bobby&#8221; was written especially for </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Dead of Night</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, and it is easily the most haunting entry here. After a grieving mother uses dark magic to summon her missing son, the truth surrounding the boy&#8217;s disappearance and sudden return comes to light. Curtis later remade the same story in </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Trilogy of Terror II</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>Mania</i></b><b> (1986) — &#8220;The Intruder&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Mania.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630557\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/mania/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Mania.jpg?fit=1200%2C916&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,916\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"Mania\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Mania.jpg?fit=300%2C229&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Mania.jpg?fit=740%2C565&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630557\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Mania.jpg?resize=740%2C565&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"565\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Mania.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Mania.jpg?resize=300%2C229&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Mania.jpg?resize=1024%2C782&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Mania.jpg?resize=768%2C586&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Presented with no enveloping story or even an ersatz host, Canadian anthology </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Mania</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> is essentially a series of episodes strung together with no glaring theme. Still, the people behind the movie — Paul Lynch (</span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Prom Night</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">), David M. Robertson (</span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Friday the 13th Part V: A New Beginning</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">), John Sheppard (</span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">American Nightmare</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">), Peter R. Simpson (</span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Curtains</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">)  — will spark some curiosity.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">In what is essentially the best of the bunch, &#8220;The Intruder&#8221; studies a husband&#8217;s pathological fear of dogs when his wife convinces him to adopt a Rottweiler. He is constantly ill at ease around his new pet, but he&#8217;ll ultimately have wished he had paid more attention to the dog&#8217;s incessant barking. Robertson&#8217;s contribution is a sharp interpretation of a classic urban legend we don&#8217;t hear enough of nowadays.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>Horror Stories 2</i></b><b> (2013) — &#8220;The Escape&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Horror-Stories-2.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630558\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/horror-stories-2/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Horror-Stories-2.jpg?fit=1200%2C600&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,600\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"Horror-Stories-2\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Horror-Stories-2.jpg?fit=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Horror-Stories-2.jpg?fit=740%2C370&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630558\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Horror-Stories-2.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Horror-Stories-2.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Horror-Stories-2.jpg?resize=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Horror-Stories-2.jpg?resize=1024%2C512&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Horror-Stories-2.jpg?resize=768%2C384&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The South Korean anthology series </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Horror Stories</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> is generally replete with high-grade scares and suspense — &#8220;Ambulance on the Death Zone&#8221; in the first film should not be missed — but its meager second installment survives only because of &#8220;The Escape.&#8221; The first and third movies in this franchise are commercially available in the West, whereas </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Horror Stories 2</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> is more elusive.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The sequel&#8217;s setup sees a pair of life insurance agents reviewing three unusual cases one night. Topping things off, they look at a trainee teacher&#8217;s peculiar demise in Jung Bum-sik&#8217;s &#8220;The Escape.&#8221; This epic entry about a man being trapped in a hellish dimension suffuses humor without skirting thrills.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>All the Creatures Were Stirring</i></b><b> (2018) — &#8220;Dash Away All&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/All-the-Creatures-were-Stirring.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630559\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/all-the-creatures-were-stirring/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/All-the-Creatures-were-Stirring.jpg?fit=1200%2C600&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,600\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"All-the-Creatures-were-Stirring\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/All-the-Creatures-were-Stirring.jpg?fit=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/All-the-Creatures-were-Stirring.jpg?fit=740%2C370&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630559\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/All-the-Creatures-were-Stirring.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/All-the-Creatures-were-Stirring.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/All-the-Creatures-were-Stirring.jpg?resize=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/All-the-Creatures-were-Stirring.jpg?resize=1024%2C512&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/All-the-Creatures-were-Stirring.jpg?resize=768%2C384&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Christmas horror entices us for several reasons. Namely, it zeroes in on the unspoken loneliness of holidays all the while creating terror at a time when people are expected to be joyous. Rebekah and David Ian McKendry follow tradition by underlining the potential ghoulish side of Yuletide activities. One of their film&#8217;s highlights, &#8220;Dash Away All&#8221; centers around a father and husband whose last-minute Christmas shopping lands him in a life-or-death situation.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The story&#8217;s mythos is intriguing, and the main character is sympathetic. Out of all the segments here, &#8220;Dash Away All&#8221; could have worked as a longer feature.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>Amusement</i></b><b> (2008) — &#8220;Tabitha&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Amusement.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630560\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/amusement/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Amusement.jpg?fit=1200%2C600&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,600\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"Amusement\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Amusement.jpg?fit=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Amusement.jpg?fit=740%2C370&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630560\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Amusement.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Amusement.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Amusement.jpg?resize=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Amusement.jpg?resize=1024%2C512&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Amusement.jpg?resize=768%2C384&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">With its magazine-ready cast and high production values, it seems obvious the soft anthology </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Amusement</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> was meant for the big screen. On the contrary, the studio yanked this one from the release schedule and sent it straight to video with very little afterthought.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The overall story is hardly sound and falls apart if you really think about it. What does work, however, are the individual stories. They&#8217;re essentially protracted set pieces where the main characters are separately abducted by a serial killer known only as The Laugh. The most singular tale, &#8220;Tabitha&#8221; sees a babysitter turning paranoid when she finds a life-sized clown doll in the house.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>Screamtime</i></b><b> (1983) — &#8220;Dreamhouse&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Screamtime.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630561\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/screamtime/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Screamtime.jpg?fit=1200%2C916&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,916\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"Screamtime\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Screamtime.jpg?fit=300%2C229&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Screamtime.jpg?fit=740%2C565&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630561\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Screamtime.jpg?resize=740%2C565&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"565\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Screamtime.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Screamtime.jpg?resize=300%2C229&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Screamtime.jpg?resize=1024%2C782&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Screamtime.jpg?resize=768%2C586&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Originally a short coupled with longer films in theaters, Michael Armstrong&#8217;s &#8220;Dreamhouse&#8221; was later added to his and Stanley A. Long&#8217;s anthology </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Screamtime</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. The British movie begins with two Americans stealing a handful of VHS tapes from a shop. Little do they know, the scary movies they watch aren&#8217;t entirely fictional.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&#8220;Charming&#8221; is the best way to describe </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Screamtime</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, a no-budget medley of kooky stories. It&#8217;s not high-brow or even competently made, yet there&#8217;s some fun to be had here. The aforementioned &#8220;Dreamhouse&#8221; alone makes the movie worth watching at least once. In it, a woman believes her family&#8217;s new home is haunted by ghosts that only she can see; the truth is far more terrifying. The story was later turned into a longer feature in 2010 called </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Psychosis</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>Fear(s) of the Dark</i></b><b> (2007) — Mattotti&#8217;s Story</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Fears-of-the-Dark.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630562\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/fears-of-the-dark/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Fears-of-the-Dark.jpg?fit=1200%2C600&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,600\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"Fears-of-the-Dark\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Fears-of-the-Dark.jpg?fit=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Fears-of-the-Dark.jpg?fit=740%2C370&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630562\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Fears-of-the-Dark.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Fears-of-the-Dark.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Fears-of-the-Dark.jpg?resize=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Fears-of-the-Dark.jpg?resize=1024%2C512&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Fears-of-the-Dark.jpg?resize=768%2C384&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The French animated anthology </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Fear(s) of the Dark </span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">is a buffet of art and imagination; no two stories or styles are alike. The only thing these overlapping vignettes have in common is their lack of color. The movie included the talents of artists Blutch, Charles Burns, Marie Caillou, Pierre di Sciullo, Lorenzo Mattotti, and Richard McGuire.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This segment is remarkable and eldritch thanks to Mattotti&#8217;s prowess as an illustrator. He achieves a truly ambient anecdote about a man remembering his time in pastoral France: a village is besieged by an unseen predator that stalks the foggy marshes. The vague ending stirs up memories of classic children&#8217;s ghost stories. Mattotti, who is known for his renowned color work and enigmatic designs, draws us in with breathing scenery and imaged disquietude.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>Nightmares</i></b><b> (1983) — &#8220;Terror in Topanga&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Nightmares.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630563\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/nightmares-5/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Nightmares.jpg?fit=1200%2C600&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,600\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"Nightmares\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Nightmares.jpg?fit=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Nightmares.jpg?fit=740%2C370&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630563\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Nightmares.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Nightmares.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Nightmares.jpg?resize=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Nightmares.jpg?resize=1024%2C512&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Nightmares.jpg?resize=768%2C384&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The four stories presented here were intended to be part of an unnamed pilot for NBC before they became </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Nightmares</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. There is no host, and the only connective tissue is an overarching theme of obsession. As dated as these stories look, they are equally freaky. Be it Lance Henriksen battling a demonic pickup truck, or a family under attack by a giant rat, this compilation is full of creepy, cautionary tales.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&#8220;Terror in Topanga&#8221; is a straightforward yet tense opener that plays on basic fears. It&#8217;s firmly rooted in contemporary folklore, but that doesn&#8217;t make the conclusion any less effective.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>Chilling Visions: 5 Senses of Fear</i></b><b> (2013) — &#8220;Listen&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Chilling-Visions-5-Senses-of-Fear-listen.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630565\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/chilling-visions-5-senses-of-fear-listen/\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"Chilling-Visions-5-Senses-of-Fear-listen\" data-image-description=\"\" wp-image-3630565\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Chilling-Visions-5-Senses-of-Fear-listen.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Chilling-Visions-5-Senses-of-Fear-listen.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Chilling-Visions-5-Senses-of-Fear-listen.jpg?resize=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Chilling-Visions-5-Senses-of-Fear-listen.jpg?resize=1024%2C512&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Chilling-Visions-5-Senses-of-Fear-listen.jpg?resize=768%2C384&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This anthology first aired on the now-defunct Chiller network, and just as the title suggests, every independent segment is based on one of the five human senses. Not every tale is as engaging as the next so one&#8217;s mileage may vary. Jesse Holland and Andy Mitton&#8217;s &#8220;Listen&#8221; documents a supposedly cursed song that kills anyone who listens to it. This closing story outweighs its peers mainly because of its urgency and mystique; the found-footage structure also adds another layer.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>The Centerfold Girls: </i></b><b>(1974) — The Second Story</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Centerfold-Girls.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630566\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/centerfold-girls/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Centerfold-Girls.jpg?fit=1200%2C600&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,600\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"Centerfold-Girls\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Centerfold-Girls.jpg?fit=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Centerfold-Girls.jpg?fit=740%2C370&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630566\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Centerfold-Girls.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Centerfold-Girls.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Centerfold-Girls.jpg?resize=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Centerfold-Girls.jpg?resize=1024%2C512&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Centerfold-Girls.jpg?resize=768%2C384&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">John Peyser&#8217;s </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The Centerfold Girls</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> is another soft anthology where multiple women are individually preyed upon by a male killer; the villain selects his targets from a men&#8217;s magazine.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Every section of this exploitative movie has the victims imperiled directly by either the main threat or some other sadistic party beforehand. The first section demonstrates the risk of picking up hitchhikers, and the final act shows the antagonist finally meeting his match in the form of Tiffany Bolling. Sandwiched in between is a story that feels the most atmospheric: models are picked off during a photo shoot at a remote island mansion. </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The Centerfold Girls</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> encapsulates the good and bad characteristics of this era of proto-slashers.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>Tales of the Third Dimension</i></b><b> (1984) — &#8220;Visions of Sugar Plum&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Tales-of-the-Third-Dimension.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630567\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/tales-of-the-third-dimension/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Tales-of-the-Third-Dimension.jpg?fit=1200%2C916&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,916\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"Tales-of-the-Third-Dimension\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Tales-of-the-Third-Dimension.jpg?fit=300%2C229&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Tales-of-the-Third-Dimension.jpg?fit=740%2C565&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630567\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Tales-of-the-Third-Dimension.jpg?resize=740%2C565&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"565\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Tales-of-the-Third-Dimension.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Tales-of-the-Third-Dimension.jpg?resize=300%2C229&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Tales-of-the-Third-Dimension.jpg?resize=1024%2C782&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Tales-of-the-Third-Dimension.jpg?resize=768%2C586&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Lackluster stories are a detriment to good anthologies. A rule of thumb, however, is remembering that for every few so-so segments, a movie should have an entry that will restore faith in the viewer. This is what happened with </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Tales of the Third Dimension</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, a direct-to-video omnibus hosted by an animatronic and droll skeleton named Igor. After two piddling stories, the movie ends on a high note.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&#8220;Visions of Sugar Plum&#8221; sees two kids spending Christmas with their grandmother. When the elderly woman runs out of her medication, she becomes agitated and paranoid. Now, her grandchildren fear for their lives as Grandma chases after them with a gun and an electric hedge trimmer. If that doesn&#8217;t sound funny enough, stay tuned for the ending&#8217;s </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">deux ex machina</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>The Dark Tapes</i></b><b> (2016) — &#8220;The Hunters and the Hunted&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Dark-Tapes.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630568\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/dark-tapes/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Dark-Tapes.jpg?fit=1200%2C600&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,600\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"Dark-Tapes\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Dark-Tapes.jpg?fit=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Dark-Tapes.jpg?fit=740%2C370&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630568\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Dark-Tapes.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Dark-Tapes.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Dark-Tapes.jpg?resize=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Dark-Tapes.jpg?resize=1024%2C512&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Dark-Tapes.jpg?resize=768%2C384&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Using a found-footage format helps </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The Dark Tapes</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> stand out even though the idea itself wasn&#8217;t novel at this point. The most successful use was in &#8220;The Hunter and the Hunted,&#8221; a deceitful story about a couple moving into a new house. When they suspect they&#8217;re being haunted, they reach out to paranormal investigators. It sounds routine, but writer Michael McQuown has a surprise in store for audiences.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>Screams of a Winter Night</i></b><b> (1979) — &#8220;The Moss Point Man&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Screams-of-a-Winter-Night.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630569\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/screams-of-a-winter-night/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Screams-of-a-Winter-Night.jpg?fit=1200%2C600&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,600\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"Screams-of-a-Winter-Night\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Screams-of-a-Winter-Night.jpg?fit=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Screams-of-a-Winter-Night.jpg?fit=740%2C370&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630569\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Screams-of-a-Winter-Night.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Screams-of-a-Winter-Night.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Screams-of-a-Winter-Night.jpg?resize=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Screams-of-a-Winter-Night.jpg?resize=1024%2C512&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Screams-of-a-Winter-Night.jpg?resize=768%2C384&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Before its astonishing restoration by Code Red, </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Screams of a Winter Night</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> was all but lost. The only copies available until then were low-grade. Thankfully, enthusiasts of regional horror can now see this Dimension Pictures anthology in its full form — a removed story was added back in.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">James L. Wilson&#8217;s Louisiana-shot film makes the interesting choice of spending a sizable amount of time with the wraparound&#8217;s characters. One of whom is John, who shares his own interpretation of the classic &#8220;Boyfriend&#8217;s Death&#8221; legend that was still popular around this time period. The same myth is notably retold in 1997&#8217;s </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Campfire Tales</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>After Midnight</i></b><b> (1989) — &#8220;All Night Operator&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/After-Midnight.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630570\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/after-midnight-3/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/After-Midnight.jpg?fit=1200%2C600&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,600\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"After-Midnight\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/After-Midnight.jpg?fit=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/After-Midnight.jpg?fit=740%2C370&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630570\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/After-Midnight.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/After-Midnight.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/After-Midnight.jpg?resize=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/After-Midnight.jpg?resize=1024%2C512&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/After-Midnight.jpg?resize=768%2C384&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Ken and Jim Wheat&#8217;s </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">After Midnight</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> has developed a small but faithful following after all these years. With its surreal wraparound and a sprinkling of familiar faces, this MGM anthology is one of the eighties&#8217; best kept secrets.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">All three segments are told during an after-hours session at a psychology professor&#8217;s house. The students&#8217; most persuasive yarn — built on the theme of fear, as is the course&#8217;s objective — is &#8220;All Night Operator,&#8221; a cat-and-mouse thriller. Marg Helgenberger works the graveyard shift all alone at a phone messaging service when she&#8217;s targeted by one of her client&#8217;s deranged stalkers.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>Tales of the Unusual</i></b><b> (2000) — &#8220;One Snowy Night&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Tales-of-the-Unusual.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630571\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/tales-of-the-unusual/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Tales-of-the-Unusual.jpg?fit=1200%2C600&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,600\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"Tales-of-the-Unusual\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Tales-of-the-Unusual.jpg?fit=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Tales-of-the-Unusual.jpg?fit=740%2C370&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630571\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Tales-of-the-Unusual.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Tales-of-the-Unusual.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Tales-of-the-Unusual.jpg?resize=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Tales-of-the-Unusual.jpg?resize=1024%2C512&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Tales-of-the-Unusual.jpg?resize=768%2C384&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Based on the long-running television franchise of the same name, </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Tales of the Unusual</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> is the Japanese equivalent of the</span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> Twilight Zone</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. It&#8217;s not always horror — as a matter of fact, only one story in the 2000 movie is explicitly horror.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">A rainy night leaves train commuters stranded in a virtually empty station. To busy themselves until the weather lets up, they listen to a mysterious man wearing sunglasses. His disconcerting demeanor is overlooked in favor of some entertaining stories; one of which includes the unnerving &#8220;One Snowy Night.&#8221; After their plane crashes in the mountains, survivors seek shelter in a nearby shack. They take turns sleeping before realizing they may not be the only ones inside the cabin. This startling revelation is achieved through the clever use of a handheld video camera.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>The Uncanny</i></b><b> (1977) — &#8220;London 1912&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/The-Uncanny.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630572\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/the-uncanny/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/The-Uncanny.jpg?fit=1200%2C600&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,600\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"The-Uncanny\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/The-Uncanny.jpg?fit=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/The-Uncanny.jpg?fit=740%2C370&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630572\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/The-Uncanny.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/The-Uncanny.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/The-Uncanny.jpg?resize=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/The-Uncanny.jpg?resize=1024%2C512&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/The-Uncanny.jpg?resize=768%2C384&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Peter Cushing plays an ailurophobic writer who tries to convince his publisher that cats are evil creatures. His first example is set in 1912; a man discovers his wealthy aunt is leaving her fortune to her pets rather than him. The nephew then sends his lover, also his aunt&#8217;s maid, to destroy the original will. Her doing so finally incurs the wrath of the old woman&#8217;s many cats.</span></p>\n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The Uncanny</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> is sometimes mistaken for an Amicus production, but it&#8217;s really produced by The Rank Organisation. Even so, the similarities are hard to miss in this neglected anthology.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>Phobia 2 </i></b><b>(2009) — &#8220;Backpackers&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Phobia-2.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630573\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/phobia-2-5/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Phobia-2.jpg?fit=1200%2C600&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,600\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"Phobia-2\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Phobia-2.jpg?fit=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Phobia-2.jpg?fit=740%2C370&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630573\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Phobia-2.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Phobia-2.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Phobia-2.jpg?resize=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Phobia-2.jpg?resize=1024%2C512&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Phobia-2.jpg?resize=768%2C384&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The success of Thai anthology </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">4bia </span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">(</span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Phobia</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">) led to a sequel that is mostly better than the first. The last story has its issues, but the four before it are a good set.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&#8220;The Backpackers&#8221; is a harrowing account of two Japanese tourists being at the wrong place at the wrong time. After they convince a shady truck driver to give them a lift, they discover his haul is nothing but corpses. That&#8217;s only the beginning of this wretched ride from hell.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>Future Shock</i></b><b> (1994) — &#8220;The Roommate&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Future-Shock.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630574\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/future-shock/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Future-Shock.jpg?fit=1200%2C600&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,600\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"Future-Shock\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Future-Shock.jpg?fit=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Future-Shock.jpg?fit=740%2C370&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630574\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Future-Shock.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Future-Shock.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Future-Shock.jpg?resize=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Future-Shock.jpg?resize=1024%2C512&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Future-Shock.jpg?resize=768%2C384&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The late Bill Paxton appeared in this early-nineties anthology that produced a tie-in comic. His story &#8220;The Roommate&#8221; is a role reversal for the actor — in 1992&#8217;s </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The Vagrant</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, Paxton was on the other end of a bad housing situation. Instead of being the hapless property owner, he&#8217;s now the obnoxious freeloader. Even though his and the main character&#8217;s encounters are overtly humorous and never scary, the segment is a small delight. Another of the film&#8217;s directors, Matt Reeves, would later direct </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Cloverfield </span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">and </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Let Me In</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>Fantastic Theater</i></b><b> (2011) — &#8220;The Loneliness of Butcher Boy&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Fantastic-Theater.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630575\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/fantastic-theater/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Fantastic-Theater.jpg?fit=1200%2C600&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,600\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"Fantastic-Theater\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Fantastic-Theater.jpg?fit=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Fantastic-Theater.jpg?fit=740%2C370&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630575\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Fantastic-Theater.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Fantastic-Theater.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Fantastic-Theater.jpg?resize=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Fantastic-Theater.jpg?resize=1024%2C512&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Fantastic-Theater.jpg?resize=768%2C384&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The biggest peril of hyperlink cinema is organically connecting everything. Self-contained stories in any given anthology is comparatively easy, whereas a movie like </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Fantastic Theater</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> has to tread carefully. What&#8217;s even more difficult is having multiple directors in charge — there&#8217;s always the risk of clashing styles and voices. The three directors in this South Korean film, on the other hand, do a commendable job of keeping everything coherent from a narrative standpoint.</span></p>\n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Fantastic Theater </span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">(also known as </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Short! Short! Short!</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">) artfully visualizes the struggle between reality and fantasy; the strive for creativity in a world dictated by money is also on display. The most accessible story in this arthouse anthology about movies within movies is the middle portion: a teenage vegetarian crosses paths with a killer Minotaur. It doesn&#8217;t all make sense, but the film&#8217;s cinematic eye candy is worthwhile.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>The Field Guide to Evil</i></b><b> (2018) — &#8220;Haunted by Al Karisi, The Childbirth Djinn&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Field-Guide-to-Evil.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630577\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/field-guide-to-evil-2/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Field-Guide-to-Evil.jpg?fit=1200%2C600&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,600\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"Field-Guide-to-Evil\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Field-Guide-to-Evil.jpg?fit=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Field-Guide-to-Evil.jpg?fit=740%2C370&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630577\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Field-Guide-to-Evil.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Field-Guide-to-Evil.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Field-Guide-to-Evil.jpg?resize=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Field-Guide-to-Evil.jpg?resize=1024%2C512&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Field-Guide-to-Evil.jpg?resize=768%2C384&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">On top of challenging subject matter and experimental filming techniques, several horror anthologies born in the last decade have been positively ambitious. There is also more diversity and crossover appeal than ever before.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">By pooling the talent of eight unique directors, </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The Field Guide to Evil </span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">unveils a wide range of folkloric stories. </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Baskin </span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">director Can Evrenol stops viewers in their tracks with &#8220;Haunted by Al Karisi, The Childbirth Djinn.&#8221; This allegorical story examines women&#8217;s domestic roles with frightening results.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>Chilling Visions: 5 States of Fear</i></b><b> (2014) — &#8220;Mutilation&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Chilling-Visions-5-States-of-Fear-Mutilation.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630578\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/chilling-visions-5-states-of-fear-mutilation/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Chilling-Visions-5-States-of-Fear-Mutilation.jpg?fit=1200%2C600&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,600\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"Chilling-Visions-5-States-of-Fear-Mutilation\" data-image-description=\"\" data-large-file=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Chilling-Visions-5-States-of-Fear-Mutilation.jpg?fit=740%2C370&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-3630578\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Chilling-Visions-5-States-of-Fear-Mutilation.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Chilling-Visions-5-States-of-Fear-Mutilation.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Chilling-Visions-5-States-of-Fear-Mutilation.jpg?resize=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Chilling-Visions-5-States-of-Fear-Mutilation.jpg?resize=1024%2C512&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Chilling-Visions-5-States-of-Fear-Mutilation.jpg?resize=768%2C384&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">In the unrelated sequel to </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Chilling Visions: 5 Senses of Fear</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, terror hits the road and travels to five different states. Amid this party of five is the very nasty &#8220;Mutilation,&#8221; a story entailing a man seeking to scatter his late father&#8217;s ashes at a campsite. He and his partner soon succumb to hallucinations where they think insects are buried beneath their skin. Inspirations for &#8220;Mutilation&#8221; are likely &#8220;The Raft&#8221; from </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Creepshow 2</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> and </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Bug.</span></i></p>\n<hr />\n<h2><b><i>Family Portraits: A Trilogy of America</i></b><b> (2003) — &#8220;Cutting Moments&#8221;</b></h2>\n<p><a href=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Family-Portraits-Trilogy-of-America-Cutting-Moments.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3630579\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/editorials/3630549/30-standout-segments-underseen-horror-anthology-movies/attachment/family-portraits-trilogy-of-america-cutting-moments/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Family-Portraits-Trilogy-of-America-Cutting-Moments.jpg?fit=1200%2C600&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1200,600\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"Family-Portraits-Trilogy-of-America-Cutting-Moments\" data-image-description=\"\" wp-image-3630579\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Family-Portraits-Trilogy-of-America-Cutting-Moments.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Family-Portraits-Trilogy-of-America-Cutting-Moments.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w,
