src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/BloodyDisgusting/~4/_Ab9sXdP_FU\" height=\"1\" width=\"1\" alt=\"\"/>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Wed, 02 Sep 2020 19:26:55 +0000","feedId":13077,"bgimg":"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/THE-OWNERS_9.jpg?resize=740%2C494&ssl=1","linkMd5":"0e5ccb8012f91b162dda9814722f10c9","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn12@2020_1/2020/09/05/08-45-26-015_c7d047f8780ea5f2.webp","destWidth":740,"destHeight":494,"sourceBytes":42738,"destBytes":42738,"author":"Meagan Navarro","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/THE-OWNERS_9.jpg?resize=740%2C494&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn12@2020_1/2020/09/05/08-45-26-015_c7d047f8780ea5f2.webp","https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/2-5skullrating.png?resize=224%2C64&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn58@2020_6/2020/09/05/08-45-57-995_9af33b59ddd56231.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/BloodyDisgusting/~4/_Ab9sXdP_FU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn19@2020_5/2020/09/05/08-45-59-925_0730a376ca248961.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1599295525723},{"createdTime":"2020-09-05 16:45:25","updatedTime":"2020-09-05 16:45:25","title":"“Princes of Darkness” Mod Brings ‘Vampire: The Masquerade’ Into ‘Crusader Kings III’","link":"https://bloody-disgusting.com/?p=3630498","description":"<p>So, Paradox Interactive&#8217;s <strong><em>Crusader Kings III</em></strong> is out to critical acclaim by numerous publications and fans. So what&#8217;s in it for horror gamers? Well, considering that we&#8217;re still waiting on Paradox&#8217;s other big game in <strong><em>Vampire: The Masquerade – Bloodlines 2</em></strong>, <em>Crusader Kings III</em> might be able to tide you over with a little help from a group of modders known for their past total conversions.</p>\n<p>The Princes of Darkness Mod, which is part of the officially-sanctioned World of Darkness fan works known as the Dark Pack, is the successor mod to Princes of Darkness for <strong><em>Crusader Kings II</em></strong>. The mod is an overhaul of the base game, aimed at bringing the World of Darkness into life in <em>Crusader Kings III</em>. As such, it revamps gameplay concepts, and uses the extensive lore of its world to present a radically different all-around experience.</p>\n<p>Everything has been tweaked. For starters, you play as a vampire. You won&#8217;t die of old age or disease, but pesky things like being put to the torch or losing your head will get you killed. As such, succession is a lesser, but still present, concern for you. Marriages can&#8217;t produce children, so they are mostly a political tool.</p>\n<p>Religions, a core part of the gameplay, represent the core philosophical tenets of your character. It also helps you to not fall to the Beast, a literal manifestation of your inner monstrosity. Being unable to do so causes your character to become a feral wight, resulting in his abdication. You can find out more about the changes in the mod via its <a href=\"https://steamcommunity.com/sharedfiles/filedetails/?id=2216659254\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Steam page</a>, where you can also download the mod.</p>\n<p>If you like what you see (and experience), you can also choose to toss a few bucks at the mod team&#8217;s <a href=\"https://www.patreon.com/princesofdarkness\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Patreon page</a>.</p>\n<p><em>Crusader Kings III</em> is out now on Steam. <em>Vampire: The Masquerade – Bloodlines 2</em> is due out on PlayStation 4, PlayStation 5, Xbox One, Xbox Series X and PC in 2021.</p>\n<img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/BloodyDisgusting/~4/BnJA_ZDn92U\" height=\"1\" width=\"1\" alt=\"\"/>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Fri, 04 Sep 2020 17:25:11 +0000","feedId":13077,"bgimg":"","linkMd5":"587f35cdbe1cc764411d5f5009cb44b7","bgimgJsdelivr":"","metaImg":"","author":"Mike Wilson","articleImgCdnMap":{"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/BloodyDisgusting/~4/BnJA_ZDn92U":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn35@2020_4/2020/09/05/08-45-59-913_5c3c0632bdf9d217.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1599295525717},{"createdTime":"2020-09-05 16:45:25","updatedTime":"2020-09-05 16:45:25","title":"New Decade, New Rules: The Pandemic Gives Horror a Chance to Rewrite the Rules","link":"https://bloody-disgusting.com/?p=3630058","description":"<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Does anyone even remember we’re in a new decade? Feels weird to say since it seems like we’re living several years in the span of a few months and, being completely honest with ourselves, 2020 waved the white flag. We get it. A once in a lifetime pandemic tends to have that effect. With that in mind, what will horror look like for the next ten years? Historically, it takes a while for a decade of horror to truly define itself, something often determined by real-world events. </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Saw</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> and </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Hostel</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> didn’t drop until 2004 and 2005, respectively, but became the epitome of early 2000s horror. Before that, ‘90s horror didn’t find its voice until 1996 with </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Scream</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. </span></p>\n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Scream</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, which turns 25 next year, famously outlined the rules for surviving a horror flick. What was true then is still true today: you pay for your transgressions no matter how big or small. Characters walk into rooms they shouldn’t, open doors that should stay closed, and play around with forces beyond their control just for a couple of laughs. And every time, without fail, something bad happens. Horror films reinforce our cause and effect belief system, giving us a bit of a false sense of comfort when the final body drops. But living through a pandemic changes every single rule. Many are suffering due to no fault of their own, and there’s no plan coming and no hero ready to burst through the door to save the day.</span></p>\n<blockquote><p><strong>The 2020s should explore what it means to be helpless. How it feels to follow the rules and get nothing but an icy embrace in return. </strong></p></blockquote>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Once again, horror needs to look inward, examine the rules, and rewrite them. How does that look in some of the most famous subgenres of the last decade? Glad you asked.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We’re in the age of small gatherings only consisting of friends and family; people we trust with our lives because we believe they value their own. Plus, those are the rules. Since pandemics have a way of making you think twice when that doorbell rings, the external threat of the bad guys in home invasion movies like </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You’re Next</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> or</span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> The Strangers</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> would have no appeal. Instead, the internal threat from anyone in those small gatherings becomes the new fear. There’s no need for forced entry because we willingly let them inside when they come rapping at our door, greeting us with a smile and the warmth of familiarity. </span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Or worse, the tormentor could be a family member who lives under the same roof as the main character(s) and wants nothing more than to see them suffer. The movie becomes a metaphor for what we’re going through and makes our safe spaces anything but. It speaks to the fact that a virus can live in our loved ones and we never really know how safe we are. But ultimately, it’s a lot scarier knowing the people we trust with our lives can just as easily decide we’re as disposable as a napkin. </span></p>\n<div id=\"attachment_3622624\" style=\"width: 1930px\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/HOST-Shudder.jpg?ssl=1\"><img aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-3622624\" data-attachment-id=\"3622624\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/movie/3622623/shudder-sets-zoom-themed-host-july-30th-release/attachment/host-shudder/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/HOST-Shudder.jpg?fit=1920%2C910&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1920,910\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"HOST-Shudder\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/HOST-Shudder.jpg?fit=300%2C142&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/HOST-Shudder.jpg?fit=740%2C350&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"size-full wp-image-3622624\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/HOST-Shudder.jpg?resize=740%2C351&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"351\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/HOST-Shudder.jpg?w=1920&#38;ssl=1 1920w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/HOST-Shudder.jpg?resize=300%2C142&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/HOST-Shudder.jpg?resize=1024%2C485&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/HOST-Shudder.jpg?resize=768%2C364&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/HOST-Shudder.jpg?resize=1536%2C728&#38;ssl=1 1536w, https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/HOST-Shudder.jpg?w=1480&#38;ssl=1 1480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a><p id=\"caption-attachment-3622624\" class=\"wp-caption-text\">Shudder&#8217;s &#8216;Host&#8217;</p></div>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Perhaps no other subgenre is more of a slave to its rules than found footage flicks. Safe to say we now have a little more empathy for the annoying person who won’t drop the camera. We’re all trying to make sense of the world in any way we can, and for the most part, that means sharing our madness with others. To say nothing of it being the only way some of us can communicate with the outside world. Because of all of that, plus the fact TikTok and Instagram are now essentially appendages, a found footage movie in 2023 will have a completely different subtext than one from 2016. </span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The scariest thing about these movies, besides whatever is doing the haunting, should be that the refusal to film and share is what will get these characters killed. No matter what happens, no matter how bad it is, no matter how ridiculous and absurd the situation gets, they must keep rolling. The movie itself demands they keep going, the entity wants all that attention, and the characters can’t live without feeding the beast. We, the audience, demand the cameras stay on as well. Our societal pressures to share and create content gave birth to new rules. If it’s not on social media, then it didn’t happen at all. If you say you were terrorized by a demon and didn’t stream it for the world to see, then you’re probably lying. </span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We’re told if we follow the rules and do the things we’re supposed to do to be thought of as good, upstanding citizens, those charged with protecting us will do so. </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The Crazies</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> and any of the 100 or so </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Purge</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> movies refute that idea by portraying government as women and men who magically appear whenever trouble arises. Monster on their block? Here come the suits. When an experiment goes wrong and affects an entire town? Suits send in the military. Sky-high crime rate? Suits implement legal murder and thin the herd. Pandemic? Well, they at least try. </span></p>\n<blockquote><p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><strong>But our reality is the flip side of that dynamic. Corruption is worse when combined with incompetence. The people in charge have no clue how to fix anything and don&#8217;t even know where to start.</strong> </span></p></blockquote>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This decade should deal with the scariness of ineptitude. Instead of seeing suits and military fatigues when that monster comes, characters get nothing. When a bomb is misplaced or a chemical experiment goes south, not even containment is an option because there are no options. </span></p>\n<div id=\"attachment_3630298\" style=\"width: 1787px\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Beach-House.jpg?ssl=1\"><img aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-3630298\" data-orig-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Beach-House.jpg?fit=1777%2C934&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1777,934\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-title=\"Beach-House\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Beach-House.jpg?fit=300%2C158&#38;ssl=1\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Beach-House.jpg?resize=740%2C389&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"389\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Beach-House.jpg?w=1777&#38;ssl=1 1777w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Beach-House.jpg?resize=300%2C158&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Beach-House.jpg?resize=1024%2C538&#38;ssl=1 1024w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Beach-House.jpg?resize=768%2C404&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Beach-House.jpg?resize=1536%2C807&#38;ssl=1 1536w, https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Beach-House.jpg?w=1480&#38;ssl=1 1480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 740px) 100vw, 740px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></a><p id=\"caption-attachment-3630298\" class=\"wp-caption-text\">&#8216;The Beach House&#8217;</p></div>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Being abandoned sucks. Being abandoned because the person or people in charge can’t handle the problem sucks even more. There is a specific trauma that event elicits; it’s one horror rarely explores but certainly should. That stress can result in people hurting themselves, hurting the ones around them, drowning in despair, or an entire society living out scenes from <em>The Shining</em>. These films can examine our relationship with institutions meant to protect us and what it’s like watching a group of people slowly descend into nihilism all because they followed the rules and were completely misled. </span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">2020 is the year a particular brand of scary movie broke the fourth wall. How can we ever go back to the typical ghosts, goblins, and strangers at our door? We know what lurks around the corner, which doors not to open, how many seconds it takes for that jump scare, and where that apparition will pop up. To paraphrase the tagline of an underrated entry in the <em>Scream</em> series, it’s a new decade, and it’s time for new rules. </span></p>\n<img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/BloodyDisgusting/~4/3bMRxy3si_8\" height=\"1\" width=\"1\" alt=\"\"/>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Wed, 02 Sep 2020 19:35:47 +0000","feedId":13077,"bgimg":"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/HOST-Shudder.jpg?resize=740%2C351&ssl=1","linkMd5":"cf5952ff81e7e0593f3da8c93611d2ac","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn7@2020_2/2020/09/05/08-45-25-864_0dfd98ef34ad4046.webp","destWidth":740,"destHeight":351,"sourceBytes":17772,"destBytes":17772,"author":"Marcus Shorter","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/HOST-Shudder.jpg?resize=740%2C351&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn7@2020_2/2020/09/05/08-45-25-864_0dfd98ef34ad4046.webp","https://i2.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/Beach-House.jpg?resize=740%2C389&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn62@2020_1/2020/09/05/08-45-59-372_96a61a18b1461ea2.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/BloodyDisgusting/~4/3bMRxy3si_8":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn62@2020_2/2020/09/05/08-46-00-763_f6e0819ed523ae7f.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1599295525723},{"createdTime":"2020-09-05 16:45:25","updatedTime":"2020-09-05 16:45:25","title":"New ‘Abyssal Spider’ Trailer Actually Reveals One of the Aquatic Spiders This Time [Video]","link":"https://bloody-disgusting.com/?p=3630530","description":"<p>We told you about director<strong> Joe Chien</strong>‘s creature feature <strong><em>Abyssal Spider</em></strong> just last month, which features a massive big bad in the form of a water-dwelling spider-monster.</p>\n<p>It would seem that there are aqua spiders both big and bigger in the film, though none of them were actually shown off in the original trailer. Have no fear because a new one has arrived today and while it similarly keeps the threat off screen, it does at least give us a taste of what these particular creatures look like. So be sure to watch until the very end!</p>\n<p>A rough translation of the plot teases…</p>\n<p>“Rescue member Ajie (played by <strong>Wang Yangming</strong>) and his companions rescued a reef tanker in the storm, but met the captain who was stubborn and unwilling to give up. At the same time, a dark shadow haunted the deep sea and dragged everyone into the sea. The surviving Ajie from then on, bearing the shadow of the death of colleagues, became decadent and disheartened.</p>\n<p>“Many years later, Ajie overcomes the shadow and boarded the fishing boat again, but he was constantly provoked by crew member Atai (played by <strong>Zheng Renshuo</strong>), deputy captain Ading (played by <strong>Li Liren</strong>) and others. One day, everyone rescued Xiaojing (played by <strong>Ke Jiaying</strong>) who had fallen into the sea due to the overturning of the yacht. Subtle changes occurred on the boat due to Xiaojing’s intrusion. Accidents began to spread frequently on the boat. Some people fell into the sea and died unexpectedly, and food and drinking water were destroyed. Because of the space pressure in the cabin and the lack of air and food, people began to clamor and panic, turning from mutual support to self-suspicion.</p>\n<p>“When the trapped people face the severe test of the storm, they find that the most dangerous thing is far more than this. <strong>There are unknown creatures under the water</strong>…The savage people must put aside their prejudices and work together to survive.”</p>\n<p>Check out the trailer and poster art below. Squires","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/the-boys-funko.jpg?resize=740%2C740&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn84@2020_1/2020/09/05/08-45-25-858_51bf7a51f4a35bc7.webp","https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/the-boys-funko-2.jpg?resize=740%2C740&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn92@2020_3/2020/09/05/08-45-58-030_de705327afc12845.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/BloodyDisgusting/~4/0JeHK7cd9_Q":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn34@2020_2/2020/09/05/08-45-58-989_8a415290a1564106.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1599295525720},{"createdTime":"2020-09-05 16:45:25","updatedTime":"2020-09-05 16:45:25","title":"‘Friday the 13th Part 2’: What to Expect from the Newly-Unearthed Uncut Gore Footage","link":"https://bloody-disgusting.com/?p=3630358","description":"<p>As is typical of most <strong>Scream Factory</strong> releases, their upcoming <a href=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/home-video/3630231/scream-factory-fully-details-friday-13th-collection-blu-ray-release-uncut-gore-footage-part-2/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><strong><i>Friday the 13th</i></strong> Blu-ray set</a> appears to be absolutely stacked with special features. In addition to the gorgeous box artwork and enticing bonuses that were unveiled a few months back (uncut <i>Jason Goes to Hell</i> on Blu!!!), a number of other supplements in this loaded collection were detailed yesterday in a comprehensive look at what this set will include. And while it surely would have been an eye-raising must-have for both <i>Friday</i> fans and physical media enthusiasts based on the numerous extras on display (commentaries, 4K scans, featurettes, marketing materials and more!), there is one particular included treat that will have longtime fans frothing at the mouth…</p>\n<p><strong><i>Friday</i><em> the 13th Part</em> <i>2</i>. Uncut. Gore. Footage.</strong></p>\n<p>That’s right, Scream Factory has unearthed this long sought after <i>F13</i> grail and will be presenting it on disc for the first time. Though they’ve cautioned that the footage is sourced from a vintage VHS tape, these deleted clips will surely be the biggest draw for <i>Friday</i> fans who likely never expected to lay eyes on clips long thought to be forever lost. Scream Factory further noted that the extra gore sequences will be presented as a standalone supplement, rather than being reintegrated into a cut of the film.</p>\n<p>So what will these long-excised clips feature, anyway? Well, according to missing films authority <a href=\"https://lostmediaarchive.fandom.com/wiki/Friday_the_13th_Part_2_(lost_uncensored_scenes_from_slasher_film;_1981)\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Lost Media Archive</a>, the theatrical cut of <i>Friday the 13th Part 2</i> that we all know and love was shorn of 48 seconds of footage, which constituted the following:</p>\n<p>1) a bloodier ice pick death for Alice</p>\n<p>2) a longer, more gruesome wire death for Crazy Ralph</p>\n<p>3) bloodier deaths for the police officer (via claw hammer) and Scott (who gets his throat slashed in a more explicit manner)</p>\n<p>4) an alternate version of Mark’s death, featuring a brief moment with Jason’s machete going into his face</p>\n<p>5) an alternate final shot of Pamela’s severed head opening her eyes just before the credits hit (given that this isn’t exactly a gore shot, one wonders if it will be included)</p>\n<p>6) finally, there is the “Jeff and Sandra” scene. Or, as Scream Factory put it in a release, “THAT Jeff and Sandra” scene. An impalement sequence which finds both characters run through by Jason at once, this graphic footage was cut from the film, even though a still of this gory death made its way into Fango and the back cover of an early VHS release.</p>\n<p>Of course, there is another facet of the Jeff and Sandra scene which is more than a little unsavory. Preceding their deaths, Jeff and Sandra have sex &#8211; a moment which depicts Sandra in a full frontal nude scene. That shouldn’t be too terribly shocking, except for the fact that Sandra actor Marta Kober was underage, being only seventeen years old at the time of filming. Once this fact was discovered by Paramount, they ordered the footage to be removed from the film. Whether or not this sequence will be included on the Blu-ray is yet to be seen &#8211; though, if one guy’s opinion here matters, I really hope it never sees the light of day. That footage should remain lost.</p>\n<p>So how exactly was all of this footage unearthed? <a href=\"https://www.facebook.com/1387381511510552/posts/2576516205930404/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">In a Facebook post by bonus content producer Samuelson Studios</a>, owner Edwin Samuelson recounts the events that led to the discovery of the missing footage. Playing a hunch, Samuelson contacted <i>F13 Part 2</i> FX artist Carl Fullerton, who had reportedly showed the uncut footage to fellow FX legend Greg Nicotero. Indeed, it turned out that Fullerton <i>was</i> in possession of the footage, all saved to a nearly four decade old VHS tape. This revelation was followed by a coordinated effort to retrieve the precious clips, with Samuelson, <i>F13 Part 2</i> actor Bill Randolph, Samuelson’s co-producer and <i>Crystal Lake Memories</i> author Peter Bracke, and Scream Factory’s Cliff MacMillan and Jeff Nelson all lending a hand to shepherd the footage along to its safe transfer to digital. There’s far more to the process than that (including the videotape being baked!), so make certain to hit that link and check out a pretty fascinating story.</p>\n<p>In addition to this adventure, Samuelson notes that “several minutes” were originally trimmed from the film, so it’s possible that we’ll see even more footage than we could hope to expect based on the previous reports.</p>\n<p>In any case, no matter its condition, the length of the scenes, or the ultimate contents therein, what’s certain is that this unearthed footage will be absolutely essential viewing for <i>Friday</i> fans, and is surely the cherry on top of an already exemplary-looking set. I don’t know about the rest of you, but October 13th can’t get here soon enough.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/friday.jpg?ssl=1\"><img data-attachment-id=\"3623349\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/home-video/3623333/scream-factory-fully-details-octobers-16-disc-friday-13th-blu-ray-collection/attachment/friday-8/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/friday.jpg?fit=1462%2C1744&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1462,1744\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" Nothing says fall better than a good ghost or horror story. From graphic novels to novels to activity books, there&#8217;s something for all literary tastes this Fall.</span></p>\n<p>Here&#8217;s what we&#8217;re recommending&#8230;</p>\n<hr />\n<p><strong><em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">The Turn of the Screw</span></em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\"> by Henry James</span></strong></p>\n<p><img data-attachment-id=\"3629263\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/tv/3629186/haunting-bly-manor-call-number-creepy-little-voice-recording/attachment/bly-manor-netflix/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/bly-manor-netflix-scaled-e1598641596870.jpg?fit=1800%2C900&#38;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"1800,900\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&#34;aperture&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;credit&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;camera&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;caption&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;created_timestamp&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;copyright&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;focal_length&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;iso&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;shutter_speed&#34;:&#34;0&#34;,&#34;title&#34;:&#34;&#34;,&#34;orientation&#34;:&#34;0&#34;}\" data-image-title=\"bly manor netflix\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/bly-manor-netflix-scaled-e1598641596870.jpg?fit=300%2C150&#38;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/bly-manor-netflix-scaled-e1598641596870.jpg?fit=740%2C370&#38;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-3629263\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/bloody-disgusting.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/bly-manor-netflix.jpg?resize=740%2C370&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"740\" height=\"370\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></p>\n<p><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">This classic 1898 novella by Henry James follows an inexperienced governess hired to care for two children at a country estate. There&#8217;s something not alright with the kids, or the estate, which is haunted by its past. It&#8217;s not just the ghosts that made this novella a classic, but the ambiguity that made the story fertile ground for analysis for well over a century. It also serves as the base for Mike Adaptation&#8217;s latest literary remix for Netflix, </span><em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">The Haunting of Bly Manor</span></em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">. Meaning that not only is this short tale perfect for Halloween reading, but it&#8217;s also excellent supplemental reading for the series.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<p><strong><em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">Night of the Mannequins</span></em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\"> by Stephen Graham Jones</span></strong></p>\n<p><img data-attachment-id=\"3630293\" /></p>\n<p><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">If author Stephen Graham Jones isn&#8217;t on your radar, this killer novella will put him there. Especially for the slasher fan. </span><em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">Night of the Mannequins</span></em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\"> tells of a teen prank gone wrong, and things get deadly. The question becomes whether there&#8217;s a psychopath on the loose or something supernatural afoot. Expect Jones to throw some brutal curveballs and for things to get extremely gory.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<p><strong><em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">Fright Favorites: 31 Movies to Haunt Your Halloween and Beyond</span></em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\"> by David J. as offer up new ideas for your 31 Days of Horror watchlists.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<p><strong><em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">Basketful of Heads</span></em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">Initially released in seven separate comic issues in 2019 as part of Joe Hill&#8217;s curated Hill House Comics line, </span><em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">Basketful of Heads</span></em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\"> is getting a hardcover graphic novel release on September 8th. Meaning that if you missed its initial run or only occasionally dabble in graphic novels, this is the perfect release to bring you up to speed. June Branch is staying with her boyfriend for a relaxing weekend when escaped criminals break in and take him. She grabs a strange ax when one of the criminals attacks her, and she decapitates him. Only his head keeps right on talking. It turns out June&#8217;s new weapon is enchanted, and it kickstarts an overarching mystery. Set in Derry County, Maine, and with references to </span><em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">Shawshank Redemption</span></em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">, Hill&#8217;s story is set in the Stephen King universe.  </span></p>\n<hr />\n<p><strong><em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">The Ghost Tree</span></em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\"> by Christina Henry</span></strong> (releases Sept 8)</p>\n<p><img data-attachment-id=\"3630295\" data-permalink=\"https://bloody-disgusting.com/books/3630285/bloody-disgustings-2020-halloween-reading-guide/attachment/the-ghost-tree/\" data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">The bodies of two young girls are found in the woods, torn apart. Naturally, the police have no leads. It&#8217;s hardly the first time a corpse has shown up with missing body parts in the small town of Smith&#8217;s Hollow. When Lauren begins having visions of a monster in the woods, she realizes it&#8217;s up to her to stop it. The closer she gets to answers, though, the more she realizes that there&#8217;s something seriously wrong with her town. Creepy small towns that are rotten to the core and a creature in the woods make perfect ingredients for a good Halloween read.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<p><strong><em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">The Beauty of Horror: Haunt this Journal</span></em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\"> by Alan Robert</span></strong><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\"> </span>(releases Sept 8)</p>\n<p><img data-attachment-id=\"3630297\" data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">For those not into the idea of taking on novels for Halloween, the only reading required here is the instructions. From the author of the popular horror coloring book series </span><em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">The Beauty of Horror</span></em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\"> comes a companion activity book that dares you to color outside of the lines this time. Ghastly Ghouliana takes you on a descent into Halloween madness as she commands you to rip up, tear out, and unleash your macabre creativity.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<p><strong><em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">It Will Just Be Us</span></em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\"> by Jo Kaplan </span></strong>(releases Sept 8)</p>\n<p><img data-attachment-id=\"3630300\" data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">An atmospheric gothic tale perfect for fans of Shirley Jackson&#8217;s </span><em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">We Have Always Lived in the Castle</span></em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">. Sam Wakefield lives in a decaying mansion at the edge of a swamp. It&#8217;s labyrinthine halls, built by mad ancestors, contain the ghosts of the past. The arrival of Sam&#8217;s pregnant sister awakens something within the manor, and a new apparition of a disturbed boy appears. A spirit, unlike any other, holds the key to locked secrets and potentially serves as a harbinger of doom. <em>It Will Just Be Us</em> offers up a slow-burn haunted house tale.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<p><strong><em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">The Autumnal</span></em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\"> by Daniel Kraus, illustrated by Chris Shehan, colored by Jason Wordie, and lettered by Jim Campbell </span></strong>(releases Sept 23)</p>\n<p><img data-attachment-id=\"3630302\" data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">Vault Comics launches a new horror series that couldn&#8217;t be any more perfect for fall reading. The inaugural issue of <em>The Autumnal</em> sets up a plot that follows Kat Somerville and her daughter, Sybil, as they start anew in the quaint town of Comfort Notch, New Hampshire, following the death of Kat&#8217;s mother. However, once they arrive, they discover the guarded town residents are desperate to keep the pair away from fallen leaves. Set to unfold over eight issues, expect horror in the form of something monstrous lurking around this woodsy New England town.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<p><strong><em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">The Hollow Places</span></em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\"> by T. Kingfisher </span></strong>(releases Oct 6)</p>\n<p><img data-attachment-id=\"3630304\" data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">After her divorce leaves her broke and with nowhere to go, Kara moves in with her uncle. While her uncle is away, she finds a strange hole in one of his walls. Enlisting the help of a local, Simon, to patch the hole, the pair discovers it&#8217;s actually a portal to other realms. Places that they probably shouldn&#8217;t go. These places are inhabited by nightmarish creatures that prey on fear. </span><em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">The Hollow Places</span></em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\"> creates immense suspense from the buildup, but expect the encounters with the monsters to get gory. Expect a lot of humor, too, offering some welcome levity.</span></p>\n<hr />\n<p><strong><em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">Video Palace: In Search of the Eyeless Man</span></em>,<span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\"> edited by Nick Braccia and Michael Monello </span></strong>(releases Oct 13)</p>\n<p><img data-attachment-id=\"3630306\" data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">Shudder&#8217;s exclusive scripted podcast series </span><em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">Video Palace</span></em><span data-preserver-spaces=\"true\">, created by Nick Braccia and Michael Monello, delivered a 10-part story involving a mysterious VHS tape and its origins. Its lead character went missing in his pursuit of answers, but not before hearing about the Eyeless Man. Folklore professor Dr. Maynard Wills, Ph.D. embarks on his investigation of the Eyeless Man here, inviting popular horror and gothic fiction writers to share their own Eyeless Man stories. Braccia and Monello edit a hefty collection of shorts that enhance the ever-growing world that began with the podcast. Look for stories by genre stalwarts like Graham Skipper and Brea Grant. It&#8217;s a comprehensive companion piece, and the mid-October release date gives plenty of time to catch up with Shudder&#8217;s podcast.</span></p>\n<img 16:45:25","updatedTime":"2020-09-05 16:45:25","title":"Officially Licensed ‘Pet Sematary’ Apparel and Accessories Coming from Vixen by Micheline!","link":"https://bloody-disgusting.com/?p=3630283","description":"<p>This new <em><strong>Pet Sematary</strong></em> collection is anything by sour.</p>\n<p><strong>Vixen</strong> by <strong>Micheline Pitt</strong> has announced an official licensing partnership with <strong>Paramount Pictures</strong> for both films based on <strong>Stephen King</strong>’s <em>Pet Sematary</em>, with tons of awesome apparel and accessories <a href=\"https://www.michelinepitt.com/collections/pet-sematary-x-vixen-by-micheline-pitt\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">immediately available</a> for purchase.</p>\n<p>Taking inspiration from 1950s bad girls, vintage aesthetic, and 80’s flair, Micheline launched Vixen to showcase her creative talents, as well as her ability to create high quality fashion to showcase the female form no matter the size.</p>\n<p>“Each collection, like the films on which they are based, has its own story to tell, and its own style,&#8221; says Pitt.</p>\n<p>“Both collections, for 1989’s <em>Pet Sematary</em> and the 2019 film, features distinct color stories pulled from the characters in them,” continued Pitt. “For the 1989 film, the character of Gage and his blue outfit have been used as the core color in the novelty print for the collection, and for the 2019 release, we employed the colors and stories from the film’s promotional art. I really loved the idea of making something graphic, but also quite haunting, and as a fan of the franchise I think we successfully created pieces authentic to both films, but also entirely original.”</p>\n<p>Pitt teases that her sister brand <strong>La Femme en Noir</strong>, which she co-owns along with <strong>Lynh Haaga</strong>, will also be announcing even more film franchise collections in the near future.</p>\n<p>Take a look at the entire collection at the <a href=\"https://www.michelinepitt.com/collections/pet-sematary-x-vixen-by-micheline-pitt\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">company&#8217;s official website</a>.</p>\n<p>Here&#8217;s a taste:</p>\n\n<a
